[0] SOURCE:
अजब जुनून-ए-मसाफ़त में घर से निकला था
ख़बर नहीं है कि सूरज किधर से निकला था
ये कौन फिर से उन्हीं रास्तों में छोड़ गया
अभी अभी तो अज़ाब-ए-सफ़र से निकला था
ये तीर दिल में मगर बे-सबब नहीं उतरा
कोई तो हर्फ़ लब-ए-चारागर से निकला था
ये अब जो आग बना शहर शहर फैला है
यही धुआँ मिरे दीवार-ओ-दर से निकला था
मैं रात टूट के रोया तो चैन से सोया
कि दिल का ज़हर मिरी चश्म-ए-तर से निकला था
ये अब जो सर हैं ख़मीदा कुलाह की ख़ातिर
ये ऐब भी तो हम अहल-ए-हुनर से निकला था
वो क़ैस अब जिसे मजनूँ पुकारते हैं 'फ़राज़'
तिरी तरह कोई दीवाना घर से निकला था

REF LITERAL:
Had left the house in a strange passion
I don't know where the sun came from
Who left him on the same roads again?
I had just come out of a journey of torture.
This arrow did not land in the heart but without any reason
Someone had come out of the pasture.
Now this fire has spread from city to city.
This was the smoke that came out of the wall.
I cried late in the night and slept peacefully
That the poison of the heart had come out of Miri Chashma-e-tar
This sir who is now is for the sake of Khameeda Kulah.
This problem also came from our Ahl-e-Hunar.
Now what is that person whom Majnu calls 'Faraaz'?
Some crazy person had come out of the house just like that.

REF STYLE:
In strange obsession with distance I left my home that day
I know not from which direction the sun had made its way
Who left me once again upon those very roads to stray
When I had just emerged from travel's torment and dismay
This arrow pierced my heart, but not without a cause I'd say
Some word from the healer's lips had found its way
This fire that now spreads from city to city in array
Was smoke that from my walls and doors had made its way
I wept through broken night and then in peace I lay
For poison of my heart through tearful eyes had made its way
These heads now bowed in search of crowns to hold and display
This flaw too from us people of art had made its way
That Qais whom they now call Majnun, 'Faraz', I must say
Like you, a madman from his home had made his way

[1] SOURCE:
हवा के ज़ोर से पिंदार-ए-बाम-ओ-दर भी गया
चराग़ को जो बचाते थे उन का घर भी गया
पुकारते रहे महफ़ूज़ कश्तियों वाले
मैं डूबता हुआ दरिया के पार उतर भी गया
अब एहतियात की दीवार क्या उठाते हो
जो चोर दिल में छुपा था वो काम कर भी गया
मैं चुप रहा कि इसी में थी आफ़ियत जाँ की
कोई तो मेरी तरह था जो दार पर भी गया
सुलगते सोचते वीरान मौसमों की तरह
कड़ा था अहद-ए-जवानी मगर गुज़र भी गया
जिसे भुला न सका उस को याद क्या रखता
जो नाम लब पे रहा ज़ेहन से उतर भी गया
फटी फटी हुई आँखों से यूँ न देख मुझे
तुझे तलाश है जिस शख़्स की वो मर भी गया
मगर फ़लक को अदावत उसी के घर से थी
जहाँ 'फ़राज़' न था सैल-ए-ग़म उधर भी गया

REF LITERAL:
Pindar-e-Bam-o-Dar also went away due to the force of the wind.
The house of those who saved Charag was also lost.
The people in the safe boats kept calling
I drowned and crossed the river
Why do you raise the wall of precaution now?
The thief who was hidden in the heart also did his job.
I remained silent because I felt comfortable in this.
There was someone like me who also went to the door
Like burning and thinking desolate seasons
The promise of youth was strict but it also passed.
Who can remember the one who could not forget?
The name that was on my mind has also disappeared from my mind.
Don't look at me like this with tearful eyes
You are looking for the person who also died.
But Falak had enmity towards his own house.
Where Faraz was not, the soul of sorrow went there too.

REF STYLE:
The wind's fierce force swept away the pride of roof and door
Those who tried to save the lamp, their home was lost for sure
The ones in safety's boats kept calling out to me
But drowning, I crossed over to the river's distant shore
Why raise the wall of caution's guard at this late hour
The thief that hid within the heart has done its work before
I stayed silent, for in that lay my soul's peace
Someone like me there was who went to the gallows' floor
Like smoldering, brooding, desolate seasons passing by
Hard was the covenant of youth, yet it passed through time's door
Why should I remember one I could not forget
The name that stayed upon my lips slipped from my mind's core
Don't look at me with those torn and tattered eyes
The person that you seek has died, exists no more
But heaven's enmity was with that very house alone
Where 'Faraz' was not, grief's flood went there to pour

इस से पहले कि बे-वफ़ा हो जाएँ
क्यूँ न ऐ दोस्त हम जुदा हो जाएँ
तू भी हीरे से बन गया पत्थर
हम भी कल जाने क्या से क्या हो जाएँ
तू कि यकता था बे-शुमार हुआ
हम भी टूटें तो जा-ब-जा हो जाएँ
हम भी मजबूरियों का उज़्र करें
फिर कहीं और मुब्तला हो जाएँ
हम अगर मंज़िलें न बन पाए
मंज़िलों तक का रास्ता हो जाएँ
देर से सोच में हैं परवाने
राख हो जाएँ या हवा हो जाएँ
इश्क़ भी खेल है नसीबों का
ख़ाक हो जाएँ कीमिया हो जाएँ
अब के गर तू मिले तो हम तुझ से
ऐसे लिपटें तिरी क़बा हो जाएँ

you too turned from diamond to stone

then get stuck somewhere else

moths are late in thinking
turn to ashes or turn to wind

turn into ashes turn into alchemy
Now if we meet you then we will meet you
embrace me like this

We too will plead our helplessness and say

Let us become the path that leads the way

Should they turn to ash or wind and fade away

If next we meet, then we shall not delay
We'll cling so close, become your robe's array
I've abandoned worship now, O Faraz, I say
What can one do when people become gods today

[3] SOURCE:
जिस सम्त भी देखूँ नज़र आता है कि तुम हो
ऐ जान-ए-जहाँ ये कोई तुम सा है कि तुम हो
ये ख़्वाब है ख़ुशबू है कि झोंका है कि पल है
ये धुँद है बादल है कि साया है कि तुम हो
इस दीद की साअत में कई रंग हैं लर्ज़ां
मैं हूँ कि कोई और है दुनिया है कि तुम हो
देखो ये किसी और की आँखें हैं कि मेरी
देखूँ ये किसी और का चेहरा है कि तुम हो
ये उम्र-ए-गुरेज़ाँ कहीं ठहरे तो ये जानूँ
हर साँस में मुझ को यही लगता है कि तुम हो
हर बज़्म में मौज़ू-ए-सुख़न दिल-ज़दगाँ का
अब कौन है शीरीं है कि लैला है कि तुम हो
इक दर्द का फैला हुआ सहरा है कि मैं हूँ
इक मौज में आया हुआ दरिया है कि तुम हो
वो वक़्त न आए कि दिल-ए-ज़ार भी सोचे
इस शहर में तन्हा कोई हम सा है कि तुम हो
आबाद हम आशुफ़्ता-सरों से नहीं मक़्तल
ये रस्म अभी शहर में ज़िंदा है कि तुम हो
ऐ जान-ए-'फ़राज़' इतनी भी तौफ़ीक़ किसे थी
हम को ग़म-ए-हस्ती भी गवारा है कि तुम हो

O life of 'Faraz', who had the fortune so divine

ख़ामोश हो क्यूँ दाद-ए-जफ़ा क्यूँ नहीं देते
बिस्मिल हो तो क़ातिल को दुआ क्यूँ नहीं देते
वहशत का सबब रौज़न-ए-ज़िंदाँ तो नहीं है
मेहर ओ मह ओ अंजुम को बुझा क्यूँ नहीं देते
इक ये भी तो अंदाज़-ए-इलाज-ए-ग़म-ए-जाँ है

बुत जिस से हों ख़ुश ऐसा गुनहगार नहीं हूँ
अफ़्सुर्दगी ओ ज़ोफ़ की कुछ हद नहीं 'अकबर'
काफ़िर के मुक़ाबिल में भी दीं-दार नहीं हूँ

REF LITERAL:

I have this pain of sadness, I am not sick.

I am not ready to get entangled with anyone.

I am not a seeker of his kindness
There is no claim of piety in Dargah-e-Khuda.
I am not a criminal whose idol pleases me.
There is no limit to the absurdity of Akbar.
I am not a poor person even compared to an infidel.

Shah Nishaan Hogi Ah Meri Nafas Mira Sho'la Bar Hoga
There is nothing that is impossible in your life.
You are in one soul from where it would be a shame to disappear from you.
Don't ask Iqbal's whereabouts, his condition is still the same.
Somewhere the traveler's head will be sitting and waiting in despair.

My anguish of love and its smart, if I speak, to whom shall I speak?
I gave my heart away myself, and now myself regret the deed,
This truth of my remorseful heart, if I speak, to whom shall I speak?
The one I'd tell would be disturbed the moment they would hear,
Then my tale of anguish and hurt, if I speak, to whom shall I speak?
You alone remain my solace, O heart weighed down with grief,
Save you, this pain of being apart, if I speak, to whom shall I speak?
If you were friend, I'd speak to you of friendship's sacred art,
But you bear me only hatred's part, if I speak, to whom shall I speak?
I lack the strength to tell my state, what condition can I impart?
And they have no time to hear my heart, if I speak, to whom shall I speak?
I see no one in reality who'd understand my plight,
'Zafar', my truth and my real heart, if I speak, to whom shall I speak?

गई यक-ब-यक जो हवा पलट नहीं दिल को मेरे क़रार है
करूँ उस सितम को मैं क्या बयाँ मिरा ग़म से सीना फ़िगार है
ये रेआया-ए-हिन्द तबह हुई कहूँ क्या जो इन पे जफ़ा हुई

ये किसी ने ज़ुल्म भी है सुना कि दी फाँसी लोगों को बे-गुनाह
वही कलमा-गोयों की सम्त से अभी दिल में उन के बुख़ार है
न था शहर-ए-देहली ये था चमन कहो किस तरह का था याँ अमन
जो ख़िताब था वो मिटा दिया फ़क़त अब तो उजड़ा दयार है

जो बहार थी सो ख़िज़ाँ हुई जो ख़िज़ाँ थी अब वो बहार है

सभी जादा मातम-ए-सख़्त है कहो कैसी गर्दिश-ए-बख़्त है
न वो ताज है न वो तख़्त है न वह शाह है न दयार है
जो सुलूक करते थे और से वही अब हैं कितने ज़लील से
वो हैं तंग चर्ख़ के जौर से रहा तन पे उन के न तार है
न वबाल तन पे है सर मिरा नहीं जान जाने का डर ज़रा

REF LITERAL:
The wind that went by and by and by does not turn, it is my contract with the heart.
How can I express that suffering? My figure is filled with sorrow.
This Raya-e-Hind was destroyed, what can I say, what happened to it?
The ruler of time, who saw him, said that he is also worthy of a gift.
Has anyone heard that this is also atrocity that innocent people were hanged?
He still has a fever in his heart due to the praise of the same Kalma-cows.
There was no city of Delhi, this was Chaman, tell me what kind of peace it was.
The title that was there has been erased, now it is a ruined day.
This is the difficult condition of everyone, this is the miracle of God.
What was spring has become a treasure. What was a treasure is now a spring.
Every day and every day, those who are bent on telling flowers, how can they bear the pain of sorrow?
When Mila Tauq was in prison, she told him that this is a defeat instead of a flower.
All the mourning is very harsh, tell me what a blessing it is.
Neither is it a crown nor is it a throne nor is it a king nor is it a mercy
The people who used to behave the same way are now treated with such humiliation.
They are tight, there are no strings on their body, they remain with the force of the wheel.
There is no tension in my body, there is no fear of losing my life.
Only the sorrows were cut, whatever breath came out, I still have my life.
What is the sorrow, 'Zafar', of your fate, which God wills, Barmala.
We have the Wasila of Rasool, He is our supporter.

REF STYLE:
The wind that came so suddenly, turned not back—my heart has no repose or care
How can I describe that cruelty to you, my breast is torn by grief I bear
These subjects of Hindustan are destroyed, what can I say of tyranny's share
Whoever the ruler of the time beheld, he said: this one too deserves the snare
Has anyone heard such injustice done, that innocent people were hanged in air
Those very believers in the faith still have fever burning in their hearts' lair
This was not Delhi city, it was a garden—say what kind of peace dwelt there
Whatever glory was, has been erased, now only a ruined land lies bare
This straitened state that all endure, is a marvel of the Lord's power rare
What was spring has become autumn's fall, what was autumn now is spring's affair
Those who day and night bloomed as flowers, how could they bear grief's thorn and snare
When collars of captivity they received, they said: this garland replaces roses fair
All paths lead to bitter mourning now, say what turning of fortune we bear
Neither crown remains nor throne stands tall, neither king exists nor kingdom's square
Those who showed kindness before to all, how abased and humbled now they fare
They suffer from heaven's oppression harsh, not a thread remains upon them to wear
My head is no burden on my frame, I have no fear of death's dark stair
Let grief be cut when my breath departs, for my own life is a burden I bear
Why fear the judgment day, O Zafar, if God so wills, then openly declare
We have the Prophet as our means, he is our helper in every affair

अब वो ये कह रहे हैं मिरी मान जाइए
अल्लाह तेरी शान के क़ुर्बान जाइए
बिगड़े हुए मिज़ाज को पहचान जाइए
सीधी तरह न मानिएगा मान जाइए
किस का है ख़ौफ़ रोकने वाला ही कौन है
हर रोज़ क्यूँ न जाइए मेहमान जाइए
महफ़िल में किस ने आप को दिल में छुपा लिया
इतनों में कौन चोर है पहचान जाइए
हैं तेवरी में बल तो निगाहें फिरी हुई
जाते हैं ऐसे आने से औसान जाइए
दो मुश्किलें हैं एक जताने में शौक़ के
पहले तो जान जाइए फिर मान जाइए
इंसान को है ख़ाना-ए-हस्ती में लुत्फ़ क्या
मेहमान आइए तो पशेमान जाइए
गो वादा-ए-विसाल हो झूटा मज़ा तो है
क्यूँ कर न ऐसे झूट के क़ुर्बान जाइए
रह जाए बा'द-ए-वस्ल भी चेटक लगी हुई
कुछ रखिए कुछ निकाल के अरमान जाइए
अच्छी कही कि ग़ैर के घर तक ज़रा चलो
मैं आप का नहीं हूँ निगहबान जाइए
आए हैं आप ग़ैर के घर से खड़े खड़े
ये और को जताइए एहसान, जाइए
दोनों से इम्तिहान-ए-वफ़ा पर ये कह दिया
मनवाइए रक़ीब को या मान जाइए
क्या बद-गुमानियाँ हैं उन्हें मुझ को हुक्म है
घर में ख़ुदा के भी तो न मेहमान जाइए

Upon the chapters of your love and faith arrived

Today you came to mind, beyond all count, unweighed
The reign of your grief has never swayed
Daily in my heart such revolutions arrived
The doors and walls of rival gatherings blazed
Whenever we, home-wrecked and ruined, arrived
Thus our silence echoed and replayed
As if from every direction answers arrived
O Faiz, the path was end-to-end the destination displayed
Wherever we reached, victorious we arrived

वो बात उन को बहुत ना-गवार गुज़री है
न गुल खिले हैं न उन से मिले न मय पी है
अजीब रंग में अब के बहार गुज़री है
चमन पे ग़ारत-ए-गुल-चीं से जाने क्या गुज़री
क़फ़स से आज सबा बे-क़रार गुज़री है

[55] SOURCE:
ग़म तिरा जल्वा-गह-ए-कौन-ओ-मकाँ है कि जो था
या'नी इंसान वही शो'ला-ब-जाँ है कि जो था
फिर वही रंग-ए-तकल्लुम निगह-ए-नाज़ में है
वही अंदाज़ वही हुस्न-ए-बयाँ है कि जो था
कब है इंकार तिरे लुत्फ़-ओ-करम से लेकिन
तू वही दुश्मन-ए-दिल दुश्मन-ए-जाँ है कि जो था
इश्क़ अफ़्सुर्दा नहीं आज भी अफ़्सुर्दा बहुत
वही कम कम असर-ए-सोज़-ए-निहाँ है कि जो था
क़ुर्ब ही कम है न दूरी ही ज़ियादा लेकिन
आज वो रब्त का एहसास कहाँ है कि जो था
नज़र आ जाते हैं तुम को तो बहुत नाज़ुक बाल
दिल मिरा क्या वही ऐ शीशा-गिराँ है कि जो था
जान दे बैठे थे इक बार हवस वाले भी
फिर वही मरहला-ए-सूद-ओ-ज़ियाँ है कि जो था
हुस्न को खींच तो लेता है अभी तक लेकिन
वो असर जज़्ब-ए-मोहब्बत में कहाँ है कि जो था
आज भी सैद-गह-ए-इश्क़ में हुसन-ए-सफ़्फ़ाक
लिए अबरू की लचकती सी कमाँ है कि जो था
फिर तिरी चश्म-ए-सुख़न-संज ने छेड़ी कोई बात
वही जादू है वही हुस्न-ए-बयाँ है कि जो था

आज भी आग दबी है दिल-ए-इंसाँ में 'फ़िराक़'
आज भी सीनों से उठता वो धुआँ है कि जो था

REF LITERAL:
Gham Tira Jalwa-Gah-e-Kaun-o-Makan Hai that was
That means the human being is the same person as he was.
Then the same color-e-takallum is in the eyes of pride.
Same style, same beauty as it was
When can you refuse to enjoy your deeds?
You are the same enemy-of-heart, enemy-of-life that you were.
Love is not absurd, even today it is very absurd.
Same Kam Kam Asar-e-Soz-e-Nihan that which was
The proximity is less and the distance is more but
Today where is that feeling of love that was there?
You seem to have very delicate hair.
My heart is happy, is it the same as it was?
Even the lustful ones had once sacrificed their lives.
Then it is the same Marhala-e-Sood-o-Ziyaan that was
Still attracts beauty but
Where is that effect of love that was there?
Even today Hussan-e-Saffaq in Said-Gah-e-Ishq
Because of which there is a wavering bow of Abru which was
Then Tiri Chashm-e-Sukhan-Sanj raised something
That is the magic, that is the beauty that was there.
Then sir-e-may-kad-e-ishq is a rain-e-light
The pasture is filled with spilled jams, which was
Then there's that good look with all your flames
The same world that was there is a blessing in disguise.
Even today the fire of separation is burning in every human heart.
Even today the smoke that was there is still rising from the chest.

That is, man is still the same flame-souled creature as he was before
Again in the glance of pride is that same hue of speech

When have I denied your kindness and favor, yet
You are the same enemy of heart, enemy of soul as you were before
Love is not dejected, even today it's dejected much more
The same faint effect of hidden fire remains as it was before
Neither is nearness less nor distance more, yet
Today where is that sense of connection as it was before
You find them very delicate when you see these locks

Even the lustful ones had given up their lives once
Again it's the same stage of profit and loss as it was before
Beauty still draws me even now, but
Where is that effect in love's attraction as it was before

Again your verse-composing eye has started some discourse
The same magic, the same eloquent grace as it was before
Again at the wine-house of love there's a shower of light

Even today from breasts rises that same smoke as it was before

[56] SOURCE:
हाथ आए तो वही दामन-ए-जानाँ हो जाए
छूट जाए तो वही अपना गरेबाँ हो जाए
इश्क़ अब भी है वो महरम-ए-बे-गाना-नुमा
हुस्न यूँ लाख छुपे लाख नुमायाँ हो जाए
होश-ओ-ग़फ़लत से बहुत दूर है कैफ़िय्यत-ए-इश्क़
उस की हर बे-ख़बरी मंज़िल-ए-इरफ़ाँ हो जाए
याद आती है जब अपनी तो तड़प जाता हूँ
मेरी हस्ती तिरा भूला हवा पैमाँ हो जाए
आँख वो है जो तिरी जल्वा-गह-ए-नाज़ बने
दिल वही है जो सरापा तिरा अरमाँ हो जाए
पाक-बाज़ान-ए-मोहब्बत में जो बेबाकी है
हुस्न गर उस को समझ ले तो पशेमाँ हो जाए
सहल हो कर हुइ दुश्वार मोहब्बत तेरी
उसे मुश्किल जो बना लें तो कुछ आसाँ हो जाए
इश्क़ फिर इश्क़ है जिस रूप में जिस भेस में हो
इशरत-ए-वस्ल बने या ग़म-ए-हिज्राँ हो जाए
कुछ मुदावा भी हो मजरूह दिलों का ऐ दोस्त
मरहम-ए-ज़ख़्म तिरा जौर-पशेमाँ हो जाए
ये भी सच है कोई उल्फ़त में परेशाँ क्यूँ हो
ये भी सच है कोई क्यूँकर न परेशाँ हो जाए
इश्क़ को अर्ज़-ए-तमन्ना में भी लाखों पस-ओ-पेश
हुस्न के वास्ते इंकार भी आसाँ हो जाए
झिलमिलाती है सर-ए-बज़्म-ए-जहाँ शम-ए-ख़ुदी
जो ये बुझ जाए चराग़-ए-रह-ए-इरफाँ हो जाए
सर-ए-शोरीदा दिया दश्त-ओ-बयाबाँ भी दिए
ये मिरी ख़ूबी-ए-क़िस्मत कि वो ज़िंदाँ हो जाए
उक़्दा-ए-इश्क़ अजब उक़्दा-ए-मोहमल है 'फ़िराक़'
कभी ला-हल कभी मुश्किल कभी आसाँ हो जाए

REF LITERAL:
If you can get your hands on it, let it be your beloved.
If you leave it, it will become your own poor.
Love is still that mahram-e-be song-like thing
Beauty becomes a million hidden manifestations
The quality of love is far away from consciousness and carelessness.
May every unknown news of his become Manzil-e-Irfan.
When I miss mine, I yearn for it.
May my personality be forgotten and the wind becomes a scale.
The eye is the one who becomes your sparkle-gah-e-naaz
The heart is the one which is full of desires
The frankness in the expression of love
If Husn understands him then he will feel ashamed.
Your difficult love ended with ease
If you make something difficult then something becomes easy.
Love is love in whatever form or disguise.
Become Ishrat-e-Wasl or become sorrow-e-Hijran
O friend of distressed hearts, let there be some redress.
May the ointment of the wound fade away
This is also true, why should anyone bother?
This is also true, why should anyone get upset?
Even in the request of love, lakhs of people present it to each other.
Let denial become easy for the sake of beauty
The head of the world is shimmering, the place of shame is itself
If this is extinguished then it will become a lamp of peace.
Sar-e-Shorida diya Dasht-o-Bayabaan also diya
It was my good fortune that he came alive.
The quality of love is strange, the quality of love is 'Firaq'.
Sometimes there is a solution, sometimes it becomes difficult, sometimes it becomes easy.

REF STYLE:
When it comes to hand, it becomes the beloved's hem itself
When it slips away, it becomes one's own collar then
Love still remains that intimate stranger in disguise
Though beauty hides a thousand times, a thousand times it's manifest
Far from consciousness and heedlessness lies love's true state
Each of its oblivions becomes a destination of enlightenment
When I remember myself, I writhe in agony and pain
May my existence become your forgotten wandering refrain
That eye alone which becomes the display of your grace
That heart alone which becomes entirely your desire's place
The boldness that exists among love's pure devotees

Your love became difficult by becoming easy to attain

Whether it becomes union's joy or separation's aches
Let there be some remedy for wounded hearts, O friend
May your cruelty's balm become regret for wounds you send
This too is true—why should one be distressed in love's domain
This too is true—how can one not be distressed in love's chain
Even in expressing desire, love faces countless hesitations
For beauty's sake, even refusal becomes an easy equation
The candle of self flickers at the world's assembly's head
If this were to extinguish, it would light wisdom's path instead
A bewildered head was given, wilderness and desert too were given
Such is my fortune's beauty that it became a prison
The knot of love is a strange and tangled knot, O Firaq
Sometimes unsolvable, sometimes difficult, sometimes easy to unpack

गर्द-ओ-ग़ुबार-ए-हस्ती-ए-फ़ानी उड़ा दिया
ऐ कीमिया-ए-इश्क़ मुझे क्या बना दिया
वो सामने है और नज़र से छुपा दिया
ऐ इश्क़-ए-बे-हिजाब मुझे क्या दिखा दिया
वो शान-ए-ख़ामुशी कि बहारें हैं मुंतज़िर
वो रंग-ए-गुफ़्तुगू कि गुलिस्ताँ बना दिया
दम ले रही थीं हुस्न की जब सेहर-कारियाँ
इन वक़्फा-हा-ए-कुफ्र को ईमाँ बना दिया
मालूम कुछ मुझी को हैं उन की रवानियाँ
जिन क़तरा-हा-ए-अश्क को दरिया बना दया
इक बर्क़-ए-बे-क़रार थी तम्कीन-ए-हुस्न भी
जिस वक़्त इश्क़ को ग़म-ए-सब्र-आज़मा दिया
साक़ी मुझे भी याद हैं वो तिश्ना-कामियाँ
जिन को हरीफ़-ए-साग़र-ओ-मीना बना दिया
मालूम है हक़ीक़त-ए-ग़म-हा-ए-रोज़गार
दुनिया को तेरे दर्द ने दुनिया बना दिया
ऐ शोख़ी-ए-निगाह-ए-करम मुद्दतों के बा'द
ख़्वाब-ए-गिरान-ए-ग़म से मुझे क्यूँ जगा दिया
कुछ शोरिशें तग़ाफ़ुल-ए-पिन्हाँ में थीं जिन्हें
हंगामा-ज़ार-ए-हश्र-ए-तमन्ना बना दिया
बढ़ता ही जा रहा है जमाल-ए-नज़र-फ़रेब
हुस्न-ए-नज़र को हुस्न-ए-ख़ुद-आरा बना दिया
फिर देखना निगाह लड़ी किस से इश्क़ की
गर हुस्न ने हिजाब-ए-तग़ाफुल उठा दिया
जब ख़ून हो चुका दिल-ए-हस्ती-ए-एतिबार
कुछ दर्द बच रहे जिन्हें इंसाँ बना दिया
गुम-कर्दा-ए-वफ़ूर-ए-ग़म-ए-इंतिज़ार हूँ
तू क्या छुपा कि मुझ को मुझी से छुपा दिया
रात अब हरीफ़-ए-सुब्हह-ए-क़यामत ही क्यूँ न हो
जो कुछ भी हो उस आँख को अब तो जगा दिया
अब मैं हूँ और लुत्फ़-ओ-करम के तकल्लुफ़ात
ये क्यूँ हिजाब-ए-रंजिश-ए-बे-जा बना दिया
थी यूँ तो शाम-ए-हिज्र मगर पिछली रात को
वो दर्द उठा 'फ़िराक़' कि मैं मुस्कुरा दिया

One who holds faith and heart dear, why should they walk that lover's lane
Without this broken Ghalib, what work in the world would wane
Why weep so bitterly aloud, why lament with cries of pain

एक नश्तर सा रग-ए-जाँ के क़रीब आज भी है
कौन जाने ये तिरा शायर-ए-आशुफ़्ता-मिज़ाज
कितने मग़रूर ख़ुदाओं का रक़ीब आज भी है
